style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(52, 49, 49);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> </span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(52, 49, 49);font-size: 15px;letter-spacing: 0.5px;font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif border-box break-word></span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb center border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(0, 121, 181);font-family: 宋体;font-size: 15px;letter-spacing: 0.5px;widows: 1;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">▼</span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb center border-box break-word><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(52, 49, 49);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">唐长安的繁盛众所周知，但它实际上是人类古代社会规模最大的城市，这一点可能并非尽人皆知。今天北京二环路以内，即明清北京城的面积是六十二平方公里，巴黎古城的规模与之相当，它们都是世界城市史上极其庞大的古代都市，然而唐长安城占地八十四平方公里，犹在二者之上。</span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(52, 49, 49);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> </span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(52, 49, 49);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">唐长安不但超过了它的中国先祖汉长安（三十六平方公里）、北魏洛阳（五十三平方公里），更是远远超过西方古代大都会罗马（二十平方公里）、君士坦丁堡（十四平方公里）。单就占地规模而言，唐长安城在全世界古城中达于极盛，直到人类进入资本主义社会以后，诸如伦敦这样的现代大都会才对唐长安保持了一千年以上的纪录实现超越。</span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(52, 49, 49);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> </span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(52, 49, 49);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">长安城的创建其实是在隋开皇二年（582年），当时称作大兴城（因隋文帝杨坚曾为大兴郡公而得名），由隋代天才规划师宇文恺设计。规划大兴城时，宇文恺年仅二十八岁。他不仅规划了首都大兴城，还在二十三年后规划东都洛阳城，后来同样为唐朝沿用。因此，隋唐时期最重要的两座都城均出自他一人之手，真是中国历史上既伟大又幸运的一位规划师兼建筑师。大兴城在唐人的踵事增华之下，终于成为辉煌的一代名城——唐长安。</span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(52, 49, 49);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> </span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb center border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 18px;color: rgb(0, 121, 181);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">城墙街衢</span></strong></span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(52, 49, 49);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> </span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(52, 49, 49);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">如果你在八世纪上半叶即“开元盛世”之际造访长安，目之所及，将是一幕幕如梦如幻的场景。</span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(52, 49, 49);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">由终南山一路向北前往朝圣这座名都，眼前是无边无际的渭河南岸平原，即所谓“八百里秦川”，背后是起伏连绵的北山。</span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(52, 49, 49);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> </span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(52, 49, 49);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">唐长安是关中这片土地上的第三座宏大帝都，其中秦咸阳在最西北端，位于渭河北岸，与渭水南岸未竟的阿房宫隔河遥望；汉长安在咸阳东南面，唐长安又在汉长安东南，秦之前尚有更古老的周丰、镐二京，约在阿房宫西南。唐时秦汉都城宫室早已颓圮，唯余“西风残照、汉家陵阙”而已。</span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(52, 49, 49);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> </span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb center border-box break-word><img class=\"rich_pages\" data-ratio=\"0.96328125\" data-s=\"300,640\" data-type=\"jpeg\" data-w=\"1280\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; width: 677px !important; visibility: visible !important; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/sz_mmbiz_jpg/jTEoOWfUwDP4QUrsXXWicPTbfoRvuPvwWibWEEN8HExAC6S6LvPpO8SFCiaWpIvOeyUME9f7Ot70egRCHMEKZfNCQ/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\"></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 12px;color: rgb(52, 49, 49);letter-spacing: 0.5px;font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif border-box break-word>唐长安总平面图。图片来源：《中国古代建筑史》<br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></span></strong></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(52, 49, 49);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> </span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(52, 49, 49);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">眼前这座唐长安城的外廓一如关中大平原，它的南面是一道绵延近十公里的城墙，高度在五点三米左右（仅相当于两层楼），全部以黄土夯筑而成，那悠长的水平线条仅被三座城门所打断，充满了沉雄、粗犷的气息。</span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(52, 49, 49);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> </span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(52, 49, 49);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">城西南角拔地耸出两座高达三十三丈（约九十七米）的木塔，那是大庄严寺与大总持寺木塔，为宇文恺所建。据说这位规划师认为，城西南方因为有汉长安昆明池，地势卑下，故特意建双塔以平衡之。然而即便是高耸入云的双塔，与这横亘万米的黄土墙相比，仍旧显得微不足道。</span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(52, 49, 49);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> </span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(52, 49, 49);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">整个长安城东西九千七百二十一米，南北八千六百五十二米，分别折合唐代的三千三百丈和两千九百五十丈，李白诗中喜用“三千”形容尺寸之大，如“飞流直下三千尺”“白发三千丈”之类，长安城正是边长三千丈的超级大城。</span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(52, 49, 49);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> </span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(52, 49, 49);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">居于长安城南墙中央的，是都城正门明德门，下为夯土包砖的城台，上建面阔十一间的城楼，高约十七米，城台上设有五座门洞。值得注意的是，明德门的门洞并非后世常见的圆拱形券洞，而是由木骨架支撑的梯形门洞，这是中国古老的城门结构样式，在敦煌壁画或《清明上河图》中均可见到。</span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, !important;\">今天难得的遗存则是山东泰安岱庙正阳门，仍保留着古制。明德门中央的大门紧闭，仅御驾经过时方开启，日常进出均由左右四座旁门，左出右入。长安城方整的城墙上，除北面设四门外，其余三面均是三门。除明德门外，其余诸门皆设三座门洞，形制低于明德门——五座门洞的独特形制符合明德门作为长安城大门的身份。</span></section><section helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(52, 49, 49);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">走进明德门，眼前是宽达一百五十五米的中央大街——朱雀门大街。今天的北京长安街宽达一百二十米，街两边的大楼大都高达数十米，而朱雀门大街两侧却是清一色居住里坊的坊墙，不过几米高。不可思议的宽度加上两侧街坊的高度，构成了极为特殊的空间体验，应该是全世界城市中独一无二的。</span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(52, 49, 49);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">长安的宽阔街道远不止朱雀门大街一条，整个长安城以三纵三横的“六街”为主干道，分别联系四面城墙上的各座城门。此外，主干道之间又辟有次干道，最终形成东西向横街十二条、南北向纵街九条，纵横交错，犹如棋盘。</span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(52, 49, 49);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> </span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(52, 49, 49);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">其中，中央大街东西两侧分别是由南城启夏门、安化门通向北城兴安门、芳林门的两条纵街，各宽一百三十四米；而三条东西向主街中，北侧的一条几乎与朱雀门大街同宽，中央一条宽一百二十米，南侧最窄的一条也宽达五十五米；其余各次干道宽度亦在三十九米至七十五米之间，而此时欧洲中世纪城镇的主街恐怕还不足三十米宽。</span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(52, 49, 49);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> </span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial !important;\">首次造访长安的人——不论是长安之外的国人，还是外国使节、商人或者留学生，大都会为这座大城为何要造如此宽的街道感到费解，然而马上出现的场面会立即给他答案。</span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(52, 49, 49);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">不知是哪位皇亲国戚或者大官僚、大将军的仪仗队，从大街尽头浩浩荡荡驶来，在行人的左躲右闪中径自呼啸而过。这大队人马竟有数百骑之多。史载，唐代亲王仪仗约六百五十人，一品官仪仗五百人，金吾大将军出行也有二百余人护卫；若是帝王祭天，则全副仪仗（称大驾卤簿）过万人，且大部分为马队。</span></section><section style=\"margin-right: helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(52, 49, 49);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">这股仪仗队过去后，飞尘无数，黄沙漫天，和你一样被风沙迷了双眼的，可能就有徜徉在朱雀门大街边的李白，回到家旋即愤然写出“大车扬飞尘，亭午暗阡陌”“路逢斗鸡者，冠盖何辉赫”的诗句。中国北方都城的大街通常是土路，长安如此，北京亦然。北京民间俗语形容京城的街道“晴天是个香炉，雨天是个墨盒”，“无风三尺土，有雨一街泥”用来描绘长安街道也同样贴切。</span></section><section !important;\"> </span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(52, 49, 49);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">王小波在小说《红拂夜奔》里对此进行了更为夸张的想象：在隋末洛阳城的土路上，由于泥泞太深，出现了专门用麻袋背人过街的“出租司机”；而少年李靖更是踩着高跷招摇过街……长安街道两旁有排水沟，并有居民组织栽种的行道树，其中以槐树居多，形成颇为优美的街景，故诗人岑参登上大雁塔俯瞰长安街市时，有“青槐夹驰道”之语。</span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(52, 49, 49);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> </span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(52, 49, 49);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">长安城大街予人的第一观感是宽阔无比，第二则是横平竖直，十二横、九纵的街道犹如棋盘，纲举目张。这是中国古代城市，尤其是北方平原城市的一大特色，白居易所谓“百千家似围棋局，十二街如种菜畦”为长安街道之生动写照。其实这是农业文明的遗产，某种意义上说，城市的街道就像农田中的“阡陌交通”，贵为都城亦不例外。</span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(52, 49, 49);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> </span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(52, 49, 49);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">长安的街道虽然宽敞气派，可以容纳浩浩荡荡的仪仗队呼啸而过，但是这样的气派毕竟不能天天显摆，久而久之，有些大街实在显得大而无当，于是有附近居民开始在街畔种菜——这岂不正是都城街道布局来源于农田阡陌的最佳例证吗？</span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(52, 49, 49);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> </span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(52, 49, 49);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> </span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb center border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 18px;color: rgb(0, 121, 181);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">里坊住宅</span></strong></span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(52, 49, 49);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> </span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(52, 49, 49);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">不像后世中国城市沿街布置商铺、酒肆、饭庄，一派繁华景象，犹如《清明上河图》，长安城的大街两旁，几乎都是高墙围绕的居住区。整个长安城被纵横交错的主次街道划分为一百多个长方形的街区，称作“里坊”。</span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(52, 49, 49);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> </span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(52, 49, 49);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">这些里坊大多由高大厚实的坊墙包围，在四面坊墙的正中开设“坊门”，居民皆由坊门出入。夜晚坊门统统关闭，整座城市实行宵禁，大街上有军队（称金吾卫）巡逻，居民只能在里坊过夜，不能上街。坊门关闭后还在大街上行走者称为“犯夜”，要受到“笞二十”的刑罚。</span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(52, 49, 49);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> </span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(52, 49, 49);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">偌大的长安城，夜晚街道上却空无一人，宋人的《南部新书》称唐长安“六街鼓歇行人绝，九衢茫茫空有月”。只有三品以上官员的宅第可以临街开门，便于官员早朝，因为早朝时分坊门尚未开启。其余普通居民只能由坊门进出里坊，于是宅第沿街开门也就成为身份的象征。</span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(52, 49, 49);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> </span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(52, 49, 49);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">整个长安城共计一百零八坊：东西十二横街、南北九纵街将全城划分为一百三十个长方形网格，中央北端的十六格被宫城和皇城占据，东起第二列和西起第二列中部各有两格被“东市”和“西市”占据（东西市是长安城的商业中心），这样还剩下一百一十格，即隋代和唐初的一百一十个里坊。</span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(52, 49, 49);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> </span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(52, 49, 49);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">据说宇文恺在大兴城的平面布局中，以宫城、皇城南面的四列里坊象征一年四季，而东西的六列里坊分为南北十三行，则象征一年十二个月加上闰月。唐开元间玄宗用二坊之地建“兴庆宫”，故最终唐长安剩余一百零八坊。</span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(52, 49, 49);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> </span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(52, 49, 49);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">这一百零八坊的大小规模不等，最大者（如兴庆坊）可达零点九四平方公里，甚至超过北京故宫，这在当时中世纪的西方已经是一个规模不小的城镇了；最小的里坊也有零点二九平方公里。</span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(52, 49, 49);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> </span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(52, 49, 49);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">各坊的长和宽规划设计得十分规整，里坊的东西长度有四种规格：由中央向两边分别为三百五十步、四百五十步、五百五十步、六百五十步；南北宽度有三种规格：由北向南依次为四百五十步、五百五十步、三百五十步（唐代一步等于一点四七米）。</span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(52, 49, 49);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> </span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(52, 49, 49);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">各坊皆环以夯土筑的坊墙，厚达二点五至三米。绝大多数里坊四面设坊门，皇城以南的四列里坊仅东西两侧设门。史载洛阳坊门“普为重楼，饰以丹粉”，长安应与之类似，各坊大门皆是二层楼阁，饰以红色，并书有坊名。坊门上设鼓，以司坊门启闭，颇似后世中国城镇中的鼓楼。坊之四角还设有角亭，犹如城之角楼一般。长安一百零八里坊，实际犹如大城内的一百零八座小城，住宅、寺观、衙署以及旅店等等，皆分布于里坊之中。</span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(52, 49, 49);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> </span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(52, 49, 49);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">坊墙以内设十字街，分里坊为四区；各区内又有小十字街，将里坊细分为十六小区。</span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb center border-box break-word><img class=\"rich_pages\" data-ratio=\"0.763855421686747\" data-s=\"300,640\" data-type=\"jpeg\" data-w=\"830\" style=\"background-color: rgb(238, 237, 235); border-width: 1px; border-style: solid; border-color: rgb(238, 237, 235); background-size: 22px; background-position: center center; background-repeat: no-repeat; box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; height: 505.381px !important; width: 661px !important; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/sz_mmbiz_jpg/jTEoOWfUwDP4QUrsXXWicPTbfoRvuPvwWuBDfpjZBW9N6cnHDPibYCftGV7zibj96pLVPHbAiaeFiaoZiaPtb8rAjvOA/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\"></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(52, 49, 49);font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif border-box break-word>长安里坊布局示意图。</span></strong><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 12px;color: rgb(52, 49, 49);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">图片来源：《中国古代建筑史》（第二卷）</span></strong></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(52, 49, 49);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> </span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(52, 49, 49);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">日本奈良时期和平安时期的都城平城京、平安京完全仿唐长安规划设计，可谓长安城的“具体而微者”，其里坊也按所谓“十六坪”或曰“十六町”的方式划分，悉如长安。长安里坊中的十六个小区内还有东西向的“巷”，以及南北向的“曲”，如同后世的胡同、巷道之类，大量民居就分布在巷和曲之中。</span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(52, 49, 49);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> </span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(52, 49, 49);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">长安的所有集中商业活动，都在两个巨大的里坊中进行，即东市和西市。它们一如居住里坊，有四米厚的市墙围绕，内部开辟井字形的主街，分市为九区，中央有管理机构市署和平准署，沿街布置各行各业店铺，沿市墙设仓库。</span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(52, 49, 49);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> </span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(52, 49, 49);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">两市的规模均达到一平方公里左右，即便在今天，也是名副其实的大型购物中心（shoppingmall）。史载东市有二百二十行，有学者推测东市中约有个体九千家，包括行肆六千余、邸店八九百及两千左右的人家。东市东北角和西市西北角各有放生池，东市中还有寺庙。</span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(52, 49, 49);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> </span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(52, 49, 49);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">由于长安城东多巨宅，人口密度不及城西，故西市较东市更加繁荣。加之西市靠近长安西门，故有大量来自西域的胡人在其中经商，李白诗曰“笑入胡姬酒肆中”，此类雇有西域歌姬进行乐舞表演的酒肆当集中在西市。而李白自己常于“长安市上酒家眠”，估计也大半是在西市有胡姬的酒家之中。繁华的西市应最能体现唐长安国际大都会的身份。</span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(52, 49, 49);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> </span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(52, 49, 49);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">陕西历史博物馆藏有一尊精彩绝伦的唐三彩骑骆驼乐师俑，在一头高大无比的骆驼背上，载着一支小型乐队，乐队共有八人，其中七名男子盘膝奏乐，一名歌姬站立吟唱，那全情投入进行演出的场景，简直堪比今天的摇滚乐队——这样热烈奔放又充满异域风情的乐舞表演，估计经常出现在长安西市之中。</span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(52, 49, 49);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> </span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(52, 49, 49);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">在东西两市附近还分布有不少祆教（即波斯拜火教）、景教（基督教的一支）和摩尼教（亦称明教）、伊斯兰教的庙宇，进一步体现出唐长安的国际化氛围。</span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(52, 49, 49);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> </span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb center border-box break-word><img class=\"rich_pages\" data-ratio=\"1.49875\" data-s=\"300,640\" data-type=\"jpeg\" data-w=\"800\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; width: 677px !important; visibility: visible !important; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/sz_mmbiz_jpg/jTEoOWfUwDP4QUrsXXWicPTbfoRvuPvwWlu8bDSNuJT8tibHDASOicwAlYheESKOqAwut6sobaFbHacnoRhE2fIEA/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\"></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></span></strong></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb center border-box break-word><img class=\"rich_pages\" data-ratio=\"0.6675\" data-s=\"300,640\" data-type=\"jpeg\" data-w=\"800\" style=\"background-color: rgb(238, 237, 235); border-width: 1px; border-style: solid; border-color: rgb(238, 237, 235); background-size: 22px; background-position: center center; background-repeat: src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/sz_mmbiz_jpg/jTEoOWfUwDP4QUrsXXWicPTbfoRvuPvwWccFmbibcdzZ5VsHfxEgwQEapI3dVnHAbxR6g24icQ1hIHYibibXrCpeYmg/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\"></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 12px;color: rgb(52, 49, 49);letter-spacing: 0.5px;font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif border-box break-word>唐三彩俑局部——沉醉的乐师，藏于陕西历史博物馆。王南 摄<br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></span></strong></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(52, 49, 49);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> </span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(52, 49, 49);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">这便是宋代以前中国城市的基本状况，城墙以内由纵横交错的大街划分为若干居住里坊，里坊由坊墙围绕，沿街不得做买卖，商业活动在集中的“市”内进行——中国古代所谓城市，即分别指城墙和集市。</span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(52, 49, 49);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> </span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(52, 49, 49);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">当然，如果全部商业活动都必须在东西两市解决，长安的生活将十分不便，因为城中最偏远的里坊距离东西市有三四公里远。实际上里坊中大都开有供应居民日常生活所需的小商铺，还有旅店之类，如文献记载长兴坊有毕罗店（毕罗大概是西域的“抓饭”）和旅馆，宣阳坊有小铺席，升平坊门旁有胡人鬻饼之舍，崇仁坊有乐器行，永昌坊有茶肆等等。</span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(52, 49, 49);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> </span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(52, 49, 49);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">从某种程度上说，长安里坊内的十字街，远比城中的大街更加富有商业和生活气息。这样的局面直至唐末乃至宋初才有所改变，一些繁华都市如扬州、长安、洛阳陆续出现了夜市、街市，至北宋汴梁（今河南开封）彻底拆除里坊的坊墙，沿街出现大量店铺、酒肆、茶楼之属，于是才有了张择端笔下《清明上河图》中热闹繁华的街道画卷——唐长安的大画家们大概无论如何不会描绘由坊墙、大街和“大车扬飞尘”构成的长安街景吧。</span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(52, 49, 49);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> </span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(52, 49, 49);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">长安城的美丽不在大街上，却深藏在一座座里坊之中。</span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(52, 49, 49);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> </span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(52, 49, 49);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">先来看坊内的住宅。《三辅旧事》称长安里坊内“室居栉比，门巷修直”。各坊之中最显眼的，首先是王公贵族的大宅第，所谓“中贵多黄金，连云开甲宅”。</span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(52, 49, 49);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> </span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(52, 49, 49);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">其中最大者可尽占一坊之地，如隋代蜀王杨秀宅独占西城归义坊，占地约五十四点五万平方米，相当于四分之三个北京故宫，庞大至极；汉王杨谅宅占西城昌明坊，约三十六点二万平方米；唐初晋王府（高宗为亲王时的府第）占朱雀门大街东侧保宁坊，约三十万平方米。</span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(52, 49, 49);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> </span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span !important;\">还有一些巨宅占到半坊之地，如唐睿宗为相王时以大明宫东南长乐坊东半为府；太平公主府占朱雀门东南兴道坊半坊，约十九万平方米。再降一等，一些大型宅第可占到四分之一坊，如长孙无忌宅占东市西北崇仁坊四分之一；郭子仪宅则占东市西南亲仁坊四分之一，占地约十三点三万平方米。</span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(52, 49, 49);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> </span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(52, 49, 49);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">史载郭子仪家人达三千之众，以致出入者互不相识，《唐语林》称郭家“所居宅内，诸院往来乘车马”。曹雪芹《红楼梦》中所写宁荣二府已是规模宏大、人物众多，可是比起长安郭子仪府家人三千、宅内往来要乘车马，真是小巫见大巫了。</span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(52, 49, 49);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> </span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(52, 49, 49);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">最豪华的室内装修手法为贴金银箔、螺钿与铜件等，可取得金碧辉煌之效果，今天日本平安后期（相当于中国北宋）的中尊寺金色堂还保留了此种装修做法，着实令人目眩。宅邸内部陈设则大量使用帷幕、帐幄、帘、床、几、屏风之类，不仅见于壁画，也多见于唐诗。莫高窟第一七二窟盛唐壁画中，面阔五间的正堂之上，主人即高坐于床榻之上。</span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(52, 49, 49);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> </span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb center border-box break-word><img class=\"rich_pages\" data-ratio=\"1.46625\" data-s=\"300,640\" data-type=\"jpeg\" data-w=\"800\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; width: 677px !important; visibility: visible !important; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/sz_mmbiz_jpg/jTEoOWfUwDP4QUrsXXWicPTbfoRvuPvwWsyQxjrk2hnJpcbMiaY4LevpYeJU8Bu6ibcjChoZXXOPbxVA2W3WUk7kw/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\"></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 12px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(52, 49, 49);letter-spacing: 0.5px;font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif border-box break-word>莫高窟第一七二窟盛唐壁画中，主人高坐于正堂中的床榻之上。</span></span></strong><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(52, 49, 49);letter-spacing: 0.5px;font-size: 12px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">图片来源：《敦煌石窟全集21：建筑画卷》</span></strong></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(52, 49, 49);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> </span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(52, 49, 49);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">汉代中国人在室内还是以席地而坐为主，唐时由于受胡人文化的影响，已开始大量使用桌、椅、胡床等家具了。《唐语林》称“明皇为安禄山起第于亲仁坊，敕令但穷极壮丽，不限财力。既成，具幄、帘、器皿充牣其中。布贴白檀床二，皆长一丈，阔六尺。银平脱屏风帐一，方一丈八尺”。</span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(52, 49, 49);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> </span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(52, 49, 49);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">唐代贵邸中最为奇特的建筑当数开元间宠臣王鉷宅内的“自雨亭”，《唐语林》载“宅内有自雨亭子，檐上飞流四注，当夏处之，凛若高秋”，有学者认为，这种自行喷水的凉亭是受到当时拂菻国（即东罗马）建筑影响的舶来品。</span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(52, 49, 49);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> </span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(52, 49, 49);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">当然，唐代官邸也有极其简朴的例子，尤其是初唐时期。《资治通鉴》载，贞观十六年（642年），魏徵卧病，因宅内无堂，唐太宗命辍小殿之材以构之，五日而成，可见清廉的魏徵宅中竟不设堂，令李世民都看不过去了。这件小事同时也是中国古代木结构建筑可以轻而易举“搬迁”的一个例证，宫中小殿搬到大臣家中组装为堂屋，全程仅五天，着实不可思议。</span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(52, 49, 49);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> </span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(52, 49, 49);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">白居易自己多年在长安为官，曾经住过三所不同的住宅，故颇能体会长安住宅贵贱若天壤之别。早年为校书郎（正九品上）时，白居易只能租住东市东南常乐坊之普通民宅，仅“茅屋四五间，一马二仆夫”而已，好在诗人“窗前有竹玩，门外有酒沽”，亦悠然自得。</span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(52, 49, 49);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> </span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(52, 49, 49);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">后任太子左赞善大夫（正五品上），白居易改住长安城东南人烟稀少的昭国坊（位在今大雁塔北），从租住民宅变为住进偏远地段的大宅，“柿树绿阴合，王家庭院宽”，但却是“贫闲日高起，门巷昼寂寂”“槐花满田地，仅绝人行迹”。后为中书舍人，仍是正五品上官阶，白居易终于在紧靠东城墙的新昌坊购得一座旧宅，一家二十口居其中，其地是“省吏嫌坊远，豪家笑地偏”，但对于白居易而言，已是在长安住过最好的宅院，大约占地十亩（约六千平方米），合六十四分之一坊。</span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(52, 49, 49);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> </span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(52, 49, 49);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">最后在五十三岁时，白居易官至太子右庶子（正四品下），得以在东都洛阳履道坊购新宅，他为此处新宅作《池上篇》曰：“十亩之宅，五亩之园，有水一池，有竹千竿。勿谓土狭，勿谓地偏，足以容膝，足以息肩。有堂有庭，有桥有船，有书有酒，有歌有弦。有叟在中，白须飘然，识分知足，外无求焉。”白氏为官一生，见识了长安中贵的连云甲第，最后仍旧欣然知足于十亩之宅、五亩之园（与韩愈宅相若），这应是长安杰出知识分子的典型心态吧。</span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(52, 49, 49);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> </span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(52, 49, 49);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">当然，不论是达官贵人的豪宅，抑或是文人名士的名园，或者仅仅是普通长安市民的小院，都是规模不同的院落式住宅而已，它们以同样的布局方式分布在长安的一百零八坊中，故唐人诗句“好住四合舍，殷勤堂上妻”，可谓各类住宅所共通之处。而家家户户庭院中生长的树木，随着年深日久，树冠逐渐连成一片，终于把下面的屋顶全部遮蔽，不论它是巨宅的华瓦，还是陋室的茅茨。</span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(52, 49, 49);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> </span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(52, 49, 49);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">登上长安高处如乐游原或者大雁塔，目之所及是绿树掩映下的万户千家，一如上世纪五十年代以前登上北京景山之所见。这是中国古代城市中万千建筑群与大自然水乳交融而成的最美的风景。</span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(52, 49, 49);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> </span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(52, 49, 49);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">李白诗曰：“长安一片月，万户捣衣声。”现在我们知道，长安城的永夜，千家万户其实是在一个个坊墙围绕、坊门紧闭的里坊之中，透过各自宅院上方“四角的天空”，来共同仰望一轮明月的。</span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;letter-spacing: 0.544px;white-space: normal;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif rgb normal right border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 12px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(52, 49, 49);letter-spacing: 0.5px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">（本文摘编自王南《梦回唐朝》，有删节）<br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></span></strong></span></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word> </section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-variant-numeric: normal;font-variant-east-asian: normal;letter-spacing: 0.544px;white-space: normal;font-family: -apple-system-font, system-ui, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif center rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(0, 121, 181);font-size: 14px;font-family: \" hiragino sans gb yahei arial sans-serif border-box break-word>▲</span><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width:
